# What are the Android settings required to enable the Truecaller Caller ID? | Truecaller for Business

This document outlines the required checks and configurations on the end user’s device to ensure Truecaller Caller ID functionality works as intended.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/get-to-know-truecaller-customer-experience-solution/what-are-the-android-settings-required-to-enable-the-truecaller-caller-id#id-1.-appear-on-top-permission-allow-truecaller-draw-over-other-apps)

1\. Appear on Top Permission (Allow Truecaller Draw over other apps)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/get-to-know-truecaller-customer-experience-solution/what-are-the-android-settings-required-to-enable-the-truecaller-caller-id#description)

Description

Truecaller requires the **“Appear on Top”** (also known as “Allow Truecaller Draw over other apps”) permission to display Caller ID overlays during incoming calls.

Below warning will appear in case the setting is not enabled.

![](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1505116975-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FyWoE7a7EzgrlGFIoECsj%252Fuploads%252Fk4oK99nMnJIRndtlJJRt%252FGemini_Generated_Image_cl4t92cl4t92cl4t.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df520ab0e-b55f-459f-a712-7dea4a3cf313&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30e2cecc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/get-to-know-truecaller-customer-experience-solution/what-are-the-android-settings-required-to-enable-the-truecaller-caller-id#how-to-do-it)

How to do it?

1.  Open the **Truecaller** application.
    
2.  Go to settings
    
3.  Check for a warning message related to permissions.
    
4.  If a warning is displayed, tap **Enable now**.
    
5.  You will be redirected to the device **App Settings**.
    
6.  Locate **Appear on Top** (or **Allow Truecaller Draw over other apps**) and ensure it is **Enabled** for Truecaller as shown in the below screenshot.
    

![](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1505116975-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FyWoE7a7EzgrlGFIoECsj%252Fuploads%252FmKu26NwkcsH1wgYyjeoK%252FEnableAppearonthetop.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a7b1341-a3ec-4a65-a1f7-496a986b4ced&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=83811e1c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/get-to-know-truecaller-customer-experience-solution/what-are-the-android-settings-required-to-enable-the-truecaller-caller-id#expected-result)

Expected Result

Once the permission is enabled, the warning message will disappear from within the Truecaller app settings, and Caller ID should function correctly.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/get-to-know-truecaller-customer-experience-solution/what-are-the-android-settings-required-to-enable-the-truecaller-caller-id#id-2.-battery-optimisation-settings-recommended)

2\. Battery Optimisation Settings (Recommended)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/get-to-know-truecaller-customer-experience-solution/what-are-the-android-settings-required-to-enable-the-truecaller-caller-id#description-1)

Description

Battery optimisation can restrict Truecaller’s background activity, which may prevent Caller ID from displaying correctly.

Truecaller requires the **“Disable Battery Optimisation”** permission to display Caller ID overlays during incoming calls.

Truecaller will display a warning indicating battery optimisation is enabled under settings.

![](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1505116975-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FyWoE7a7EzgrlGFIoECsj%252Fuploads%252FOnuPYwRlQ3h1QZhsZV5c%252FBatterywarning.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f2229b5-1537-4934-8945-b8c37e90795f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5de94e4e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/get-to-know-truecaller-customer-experience-solution/what-are-the-android-settings-required-to-enable-the-truecaller-caller-id#how-to-do-it-1)

How to do it?

1.  Tap **Disable battery optimization** within the Truecaller app.
    
2.  When prompted, select **Allow**.
    

![](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1505116975-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FyWoE7a7EzgrlGFIoECsj%252Fuploads%252FzpvcXSAfC31eT3ARFPov%252FAllowbattery.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D285f298c-288d-440e-b3d8-ea6e2a19b5ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d8b2a7&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/get-to-know-truecaller-customer-experience-solution/what-are-the-android-settings-required-to-enable-the-truecaller-caller-id#expected-result-1)

Expected Result

The battery optimization warning will be removed, and Caller ID will function without interference.

![](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1505116975-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FyWoE7a7EzgrlGFIoECsj%252Fuploads%252FTvm1y6RGwWEuHKDEXpl6%252FNobatterywarning.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7352b7df-e1f6-4b1d-b7d3-b866f18bca71&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=68b7e9d9&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/get-to-know-truecaller-customer-experience-solution/what-are-the-android-settings-required-to-enable-the-truecaller-caller-id#default-dialer-warning-informational)

Default Dialer Warning (Informational)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Description** You may see a warning "Set Truecaller as default dialer" prompting you to set Truecaller as the default dialer.

![](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1505116975-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FyWoE7a7EzgrlGFIoECsj%252Fuploads%252Fk8PSAufgw6yFg5ZzL2SQ%252FDefaultDialerwarning.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2812bd91-3fe1-4982-8dd4-0fac795586e9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3df29ce1&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/get-to-know-truecaller-customer-experience-solution/what-are-the-android-settings-required-to-enable-the-truecaller-caller-id#impact)

Impact

This setting does not impact Caller ID functionality.

*   The warning can be safely ignored.

[NextCan I use virtual numbers?chevron-right](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/get-to-know-truecaller-customer-experience-solution/can-i-use-virtual-numbers)

# Does the Verified Business Caller ID work on all telco networks, phones and OS platforms? | Truecaller for Business

Yes, Verified Business Caller ID works on all devices that support the Truecaller application, i.e. Android and iOS. It works across all devices within these OS, and it is a network-agnostic solution.

# Managing Feature Sets | Truecaller for Business

The Feature Set listing page is your central workspace for managing all day-to-day operations related to your feature sets. You now get a consolidated view where you can quickly access, review, and manage everything in one place, instead of navigating through multiple layers of the organisation structure.

From this page, you can:

*   View all your feature sets in a clean, organised table
    
*   See important details like Caller ID type, listed numbers, active features, and last updated information
    
*   Perform key actions such as viewing stats, archiving, deleting, or copying the feature set ID
    
*   Search and filter feature sets to find what you need faster
    
*   Create new feature sets through a simplified, guided workflow
    

This page gives you a faster, more intuitive way to handle your daily tasks, whether you're listing numbers, updating features, or reviewing analytics, ensuring smoother operations with fewer clicks.

[PreviousHow can I enable Secure Call for my business?chevron-left](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/features/secure-calls/how-can-i-enable-secure-call-for-my-business)

# How do I list phone numbers using Manage Listing? | Truecaller for Business

1.  From the “Operations” page on your console, navigate to “Manage Listing”, on the top right corner.
    
2.  Select the "List numbers" option from the drop down menu.
    
3.  A right sidebar modal will open with options to select Department, Operations, Process, Subprocess, and Feature Sets for which you wish to list more numbers.
    
4.  Upload your list of numbers as a CSV file. Note that your CSV file should not exceed 2MB.
    
5.  You will see two options for your file - Rewrite and Append.
    
    1.  Rewrite: This action will delist your existing numbers from any of the feature sets that you have access to including priority badged numbers and add the list of new numbers uploaded in the CSV.
        
    2.  Append: This action will list your new numbers from the CSV along with the existing numbers for your selected feature set.
        
    
6.  Click the "Publish" button to submit.
    
7.  Numbers will be validated, and successfully formatted numbers will be listed.
    

![](https://docs.truecaller.com/truecaller-for-business/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1505116975-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FyWoE7a7EzgrlGFIoECsj%252Fuploads%252FXhunSdjUtAL4h9s4KT4F%252FTruecaller%2520for%2520Business%2520%281%29.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0ce053c1-275b-44fd-8a1f-0832b91a18bc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=603292c0&sv=2)
